# Retrieve a list of provinces with query builder

### URL

```text
api/v1/provinces
```

### Method

```text
GET
```
### Note

```text

```
### Auth required

```text
Yes
```

### Headers

```text
Content-Type: application/json
Accept: application/json
Authorization: Bearer ******************
```
